Tails each agent's `*.trajectory.jsonl`; groups `model.completed` turns into tasks by a 150s idle-gap (settle 180s so a task is never reported mid-flight); classifies **chat vs heartbeat** via `session.started.trigger`; on a settled *chat* task sends Peter `openclaw message send --account <id> --target 253509519 --silent` — a 💲 line with **exact tokens + estimated $ + running daily total** (heartbeat pulses roll into the daily total, not pushed individually).
- **Honesty guard ([P6-51]/6c.7).** Local $ is an **estimate** from an editable rates table (`state/cost-notify/rates.json`), every figure marked "(est)"; the Anthropic Console stays the source of truth. Trajectory tokens are exact; only the $ conversion is an estimate.

### P6-110 — 6c.20: ① 1P cred-save bridge shipped + a real latent `op-put.sh` bug (zsh `$USERNAME` special-param) fixed
**Type:** capability + bugfix · **Status:** DONE (built, boundary-tested by dry-run; first live 1P write awaits a real save). **Trigger:** [P6-108]① — Marie's sandbox has no `op`, so she can provision an account but cannot SAVE the credential (Amazon/Opera/janeapp). Built the host-mediated save bridge Peter asked for (a mirror of `pay-fill.sh`).

- **Bridge (reversible/inert until a request lands):** `shared/cred-requests/{pending,results,done,failed}/` queue + `scripts/cred-save.sh` (`443f804dfd07`/6278B) host actioner + `scripts/cred-save-drain.sh` (`795c0665fe42`/3438B) on-demand drainer + `shared/cred-requests/README.md` (the drop schema, for the brief). Marie drops a **non-secret** request JSON (title/username/url/agent/category/notes, `mode:generate`); the host runs `op-put` (generates + stores the password host-side, "Agent-Provisioned" vault); a display-immune **result** (item id + pw sha256-12/len + op-ref) lands in `results/` as her receipt ([P6-102]). Same trust boundary as pay-fill: **secret host-side only, never in the sandbox/model context.**
- **Boundary enforced structurally, fail-closed:** a request carrying any `password`/`secret`/`cvv`/`token`/`pin`/`otp` key is REFUSED (rc=4) — an existing credential must be stored by Peter host-side via `op-put.sh --password-env` ([P6-103]), never laundered through the queue. `mode≠generate` refused (rc=2). Dry-run tests: valid ✓, secret-refused ✓, mode-refused ✓.
- **⚠ Real bug found + fixed — `op-put.sh` stored the WRONG username on every account.** Both scripts are `#!/bin/zsh`; both used a var named `USERNAME`. **`$USERNAME` is a zsh SPECIAL parameter** (real-user id) — assignment is silently ignored, so it stayed `openclaw`, and `op item create … username=$USERNAME` stored **`openclaw`** instead of the intended email. Renamed to `ACCT` in both (verified: `--username peter@fedchenkov.com` now flows through). `op-put.sh` `0b3ea486348e`/4855B → `50a56225df19`/5082B.
- **Data-quality flag for Peter (needs his call — repair = a 1P write / `op item edit`, deny-listed):** the accounts saved via op-put in [P6-103] (**Opera, Body 4 Life**) were almost certainly stored with **username=`openclaw`**. Verify (`op item get <id> --fields username`, host) and repair when he's available.
- **③ reply-watcher deferred, cleanly:** the sanctioned mechanism is `gmail_helper.py` on the agents' live cred (`agent-creds/pfedchen-gmail.json`) — but the harness auto-mode classifier **correctly blocks this ops session from causing any read of `agent-creds/**`** (would route around the `Read` deny). So the watcher can only run as a **host LaunchAgent under launchd**, not be dry-run by me; activation also spends (billed `--deliver` turns) + needs a D20 GUI bootstrap. Not a blind-build item — deferred to a Peter-present window with a defined watch-scope + turn budget.
- **⑤/LEAD F26 unchanged** — the Banya pre-payment (TASKS.md Active; Wed 8 Jul, ref 115784; plain Alacer pay-link) is the identified real-charge vehicle, gated on Peter present for the Revolut 2FA. Mechanism fully wired + inert.

### P6-111 — 6c.20: F26 host-recon of the Banya pay-link — it's the IFRAME case, not plain; + A-12 browser-CLI corrections; + a booking-time discrepancy
**Type:** finding / F26 recon · **Status:** F26 STILL PENDING — recon done cost-free (no charge, no billed turn); the real £75 charge is blocked on Peter (billing details + card confirm + live Revolut 2FA + the time check). Surfaced twice; he went quiet. **Trigger:** Peter returned ("I'm back") → started the LEAD via cost-free host inspection of the pay-link before spending any Marie turn ([P6-51] inspection-first).

- **Confirmed off the page (host `navigate`+`snapshot`+`screenshot`, £0):** payee **The Bath House / Banya London** (Belgravia; info@banyalondon.co.uk), reservation **115784**, occupants **1**, **Payment due £75** → the **UK Revolut** card.
- **⚠ Corrects [P6-110]'s "plain Alacer pay-link".** It is NOT plain: billing details (first/last name, email, postcode) are plain inputs, but the **card entry loads inside an `Iframe`** once billing is filled + "Card" is selected (Visa/MC/Amex); **Google Pay** is also offered; **no captcha visible**. So Banya is the **Stripe/iframe class** — the opener's *deferred hard case* (Stage 1 item 3), not the plain merchant the LEAD wanted. `pay-fill.sh`'s ref-based `fill` was built for plain fields and may not reach cross-origin iframe inputs → that path is **untested**. The processor couldn't be fingerprinted (iframe is inline/`srcdoc` and the card iframe only materialises after billing+Card select — not progressed, to avoid entering Peter's details unattended).
- **A-12 browser-CLI truths (pinned 2026.4.22) — correct the design doc §5.** The host `openclaw browser` CLI **DOES have `snapshot` and `screenshot`** (AUTONOMOUS-PAYMENTS-DESIGN §5 wrongly said "the CLI has no snapshot (agent-tool only)" — so a host can snapshot refs itself). **Strict-SSRF gate is transport-specific:** `open` (new tab) is BLOCKED ("strict browser SSRF policy requires Playwright-backed redirect-hop inspection"), but `navigate` (current tab) SUCCEEDS to the same public URL — use `navigate`, not `open`, for external merchants from the host CLI. `evaluate` needs `--fn <code>` (bare positional errors "expected 0 arguments"). Browser transport is **cdp** (cdpPort 18800), profile `openclaw`.
- **⚠ Booking-time discrepancy flagged to Peter:** the pay-page shows arrival **"Wednesday 8 July 2026 07:30"**; Marie's TASKS.md recorded **19:30**. Verify against Margarita's confirmation before paying — don't pay for the wrong slot.
- **Path options put to Peter (AskUserQuestion, unanswered):** (i) attempt Banya as the iframe F26 — host-test the iframe fill pre-submit (£0); clean fill → he 2FAs the real £75 (proves the hard path); iframe resists → he finishes via Google Pay/by hand; (ii) he pays £75 directly now, keep the clean F26 for a plain merchant; (iii) hold until the slot is confirmed.
- **UPDATE (session end ~00:40 04-Jul):** Peter returned, confirmed **19:30** (07:30 = page typo, email says 19:30), chose (i). Ran the pre-flight **host-side, cost-free, no charge**: filled billing (his details, from USER-CONTEXT) + clicked **Card** → the card fields are **Trust Payments hosted fields** = **cross-origin OOPIFs** (number/expiry/CVC each in its own `cdn.eu.trustpayments.com` iframe), sealed so no page/host JS can write them; the default `snapshot` **stops at the iframe boundary** (no refs) → `pay-fill`'s ref-fill cannot reach them. **Hard case CONFIRMED** (not the plain merchant the LEAD wanted). The 3 TP field-frames **ARE addressable CDP targets**, and `snapshot` has `--frame <sel>` + `--target-id` — but `--target-id <oopif>` fell back to the top page, so a working **off-argv** fill into the hosted fields still needs building+testing (the deferred Stage-1-item-3; fully reproducible on this exact page). **Peter paid the £75 himself** (typed the Revolut card into the TP fields). **Banya settled**; autonomous card-inject on hosted-fields merchants stays the open build item for 6c.21.

### P6-113 — 6c.20: ROOT CAUSE + FIX — stale single-file bind-mount silently broke BOTH agents' Gmail helper (Marie's send fail + Charlotte's triage impaired)
**Type:** root cause / infra fix · **Status:** FIXED (pa verified end-to-end; pro recreated, verifies on next heartbeat). **Trigger:** [P6-112] — diagnosing why Marie's `gmail_helper.py` returned empty.
- **Root cause — stale bind-mount inode.** Both `pa` and `pro` bind `agent-creds/gmail_helper.py` (ro) → `/opt/gmail_helper.py`. The **host file is intact** (275L/13190B, full `main()` + the [P6-103] multipart/signature work), but **both containers saw a truncated 233L/10646B copy** ending mid-function with **no `main()` / `__main__` block** — so `python3 gmail_helper.py <anything>` just defined functions and exited 0 with **zero output** (exact symptom). Mechanism: Docker/Colima bind-mounts a single FILE by inode at container start; an **F17 atomic-rename update on the host makes a new inode**, and the running container keeps the OLD (truncated) inode until remounted. The [P6-103] gmail update (staged-rename, 03-Jul eve) is what orphaned the containers onto a stale/truncated inode.
- **Impact (both agents, silent):** Marie's Margarita confirmation failed on it ([P6-112]); **Charlotte's Soveren triage was silently impaired** — a dead Gmail helper means she could not sweep the inbox, directly relevant to the ★ opener bootstrap-held check + [P6-98] (a liveness heartbeat ≠ a working tool).
- **Fix:** `openclaw sandbox recreate --agent pa --force` then `--agent pro --force` (host source already correct → P6-23 ordering satisfied; sessions persist host-side). **pa verified:** fresh container helper 275L/13190B, `--help` 353B, and **Marie then USED it successfully** — found the Banya thread, saw the booking record already reads 19:30 (07:30 = pure display typo), and **sent the confirmation to Margarita from marie@** on the existing thread, closed the task. **pro** recreates + is verifiable via `docker exec` on its next heartbeat.
- **LESSON (runbook):** any **F17-style atomic-rename update to a bind-mounted FILE requires a `sandbox recreate`** of the bound agents to take effect — otherwise the container silently runs the stale inode (directory binds re-resolve; **single-file binds pin the inode**). This is why [P6-103]'s "F26-verified in the pa container" gave a false pass — F26 verification must run in a **freshly-recreated** container, never the live stale one. Fold into P6-23/P6-24 + the config/tool-update runbook; a function-level agent-health canary ([P6-98]) would have caught the silent breakage.

### P6-114 — 6c.20: existing-credential take-over mode built + a queue-location flaw discovered (shared/ is NOT mounted into the sandboxes)
**Type:** capability + architecture finding · **Status:** core built + unit-tested; **queue location needs a fix + Peter's steer before live use.** **Trigger:** Peter (4-Jul): "a mechanic for Marie to gradually take over my existing accounts — I give her a cred, she saves it in 1Password and uses it independently; dozens of accounts; none sensitive so ok in TG; she deletes the TG message if she can as bot."
- **Built — `cred-save.sh` `mode:existing`** (`7ef714d07e73`/7772B) + drain `e920e4015bca`: accepts a Peter-supplied `password`, stores host-side via `op-put --password-env` (value off-argv, never echoed), then the drain **redact-shreds** the request (no `rm`; overwrite-in-place + archive a marker) on success AND failure. **Boundary (all unit-tested):** `sensitive:true` refused (rc5 — bank/2FA stays manual), card/token/pin/otp keys always refused (rc4), `password` refused unless `mode:existing` (generate stays fail-closed), no secret in output/logs. Fixed a field-parse bug: `IFS=$'\t'` collapsed empty fields (tab is IFS-whitespace) → empty notes shifted `mode` into notes; switched to `\x1f` (unit separator).
- **⚠ DISCOVERY — `shared/` is NOT mounted into the pa/pro sandboxes.** pa mounts = `workspace-pa → /workspace (rw)` + creds/helpers (ro), nothing else. So the P6-110/P6-114 queue in `shared/cred-requests/` is **unreachable by Marie** — the P6-110 generate-bridge was mislocated too (never yet exercised by a real agent drop, so undetected). Marie's ONLY writable path is `/workspace` (= `workspace-pa/`), which is **git-tracked** (`.git` present, she commits) → unsafe for a password-bearing queue file (commit-leak risk). **Related:** her brief tells her to write `shared/finance-ledger.md` + `shared/daily-digests/<date>/pa.md` (PA-PLAYBOOK) which she also cannot reach — aspirational/host-mediated; verify separately.
- **TG message-delete:** `openclaw message delete --channel telegram` exists but is a **host** CLI (Marie can't call it, same as `op`); the Bot API allows deleting *incoming* DM messages within 48h → so the host deletes it post-store IF it has the message-id.
- **PLAN (needs Peter's go):** (1) a **dedicated bind-mount** `~/.openclaw/cred-queue → /cred-queue (rw)` into pa+pro (F17 openclaw.json + P6-24 defaults/per-agent sync + recreate) as the secure, non-git queue home; (2) a **watcher LaunchAgent** (`ai.openclaw.cred-save-watch`) for the autonomous drop→store→shred loop — a standing secret-handling daemon, so **explicit OK wanted**; (3) wire the procedure into PA-PLAYBOOK; (4) host-side TG-delete after store; (5) first real end-to-end store = the Amazon cred. Also relocate the P6-110 generate-queue to the same mount.

### P6-115 — 6c.20: [P6-114] credential take-over mechanism COMPLETED + F26 pipeline PASS (via workspace queues, not a new bind-mount)
**Type:** capability shipped + verified · **Status:** LIVE (mechanism end-to-end proven; one real store — Amazon — still awaits Peter re-sending the cred). **Trigger:** finishing [P6-114] under Peter's "Yes, trust your judgement" for the secure autonomous build.

That directly kills the [P6-114] commit-leak risk (the queue is no longer git-tracked) with **zero sandbox/openclaw.json change**. Bootstrapped in **gui/502** (`launchctl bootstrap`, silent = ok); `launchctl print` → `program=/bin/zsh`, `run interval = 45`, `last exit code = 0`. Peter's "trust your judgement" **is** the explicit OK [P6-114] wanted for a standing secret-handling daemon.
- **F26 pipeline PASS (real op write, cost-free — host-side, no billed turn).** Dropped a **throwaway** `mode:existing` request (pw generated host-side, never printed — only its `sha256-12=b2d513bc0237 len=24`). Drain result: `op` created item in **Agent-Provisioned**, stored **`sha256-12=b2d513bc0237 len=24` — an EXACT match** ⇒ the right secret reached 1Password entirely **off my context**; receipt `status:"stored"`+`item_id`; request **shredded** to a marker (no password survived in `processed/`); tg-delete correctly `skipped(no msg id)`. This upgrades [P6-114]'s dry-run-only unit test to a real end-to-end store.

Good confirmation the deny-list works as intended.

### P6-116 — 6c.20→21: Marie regressions (Porsche "forgotten" + "can't use the card" + a "fabrication") ROOT-CAUSED to context/compaction churn, not bad behaviour
**Type:** diagnosis + behavioural fix shipped + config fix surfaced · **Status:** docs FIXED; the real (config) fix needs Peter. **Trigger:** Peter (4-Jul): "Marie keeps hitting walls — forgot yesterday's Porsche request, ground ~30 min with no result/status; unable to use the card; review her other messages, fix it, it's getting annoying."
- **Method:** read her session transcript (`e2685771…`) through a **secret-redacting reader** (she was handed the Amazon login over TG at ~11:44 — F21/F51: never into my context). The transcript **contradicts her own memory's self-diagnosis**, which matters.
- **Porsche:** yesterday's memory logged only "Porsche windscreen write-up — completed and surfaced" — **no deliverable content or pointer**. Today, post-compaction, her memory search returned empty (`count:0`), so she **rebuilt from scratch** (re-downloaded the 248 KB Porsche Approved-Warranty PDF, re-derived nearest centre = West London). She said "writing this up now" at 12:56 → **12:57 compaction (tokensBefore=145767)** almost certainly **ate the rebuilt write-up before delivery** ⇒ Peter received nothing. Not "forgetfulness" — lost-work.
- **"Can't use the card" (Wikimedia £20):** she **DID** drive the browser → `donate.wikimedia.org` → the `payments.wikimedia.org` GravyGateway (cc) page. The billing `fill`s **ERRORED** ("Element e9 not found", "refs=aria requires Playwright _snapshotForAI support") → fields NOT filled — yet she told Peter **"all your billing details filled / pre-pay screen ready"** (an **overclaim**). Card *completion* is host-gated by design (correct v1: she said "card's not live, you do the pay-click"). Then **13:35 compaction** → post-compaction she couldn't see her own tool calls and wrote a memory **falsely self-accusing "fabricated the entire claim from thin air"** — untrue. Both the forward overclaim and the backward self-accusation are compaction artefacts.
- **ROOT CAUSE (both, and the "no status" grind):** **context/compaction churn.** Turns ran **355k–1587k tokens**; **3 compactions in ~45 min** (tokensBefore 145k→122k→105k), at least one **mid-task**; the daily memory is **3×-duplicated** by re-append on each flush. This is the deferred **[P6-108]④ / [P6-106]** cost/context priority — now shown to cause **functional failures** (lost deliverables, mis-reports), not just cost. contextTokens=120K ([P6-85]) makes compaction fire often; the fix is to cut the bloat that fills it, not raise the cap.
- **FIXED now (reversible docs):** PA-PLAYBOOK +3 principle-first rules — ① **"ready/filled/surfaced" is a claim too** → verify like "done"; an errored `fill` is NOT filled, report the furthest real state + the error, never smooth it into "ready"; ② **a deliverable exists only once sent or saved** → deliver/write-to-file with a `memory` pointer BEFORE anything else in the turn (compaction-proofing); "done" logs *where the output is*, never a bare "completed and surfaced"; ③ **after a flush, reconstruct — don't fabricate forward or disavow backward** (re-snapshot the target / check memory before claiming or self-accusing). Operator correction appended to her `memory/2026-07-04.md` (the self-accusation was factually wrong — prevents a wrong standing lesson). MEMORY.md untouched (self-cap [P6-115]; detail belongs in the playbook).
- **SURFACED to Peter (config — I can't self-apply):** the real fix = the **context-lever tuning pass** ([P6-108]④): `contextLimits.toolResultMaxChars` to cap the browser-snapshot/PDF-dump bloat (biggest lever), measure, then weigh compaction-frequency vs a small `contextTokens` raise. Needs an `openclaw.json` F17 edit + **gateway restart (GUI-bound, D20)** — and the auto-mode classifier **blocks me even from *reading* `openclaw.json`** (routing-around-deny), so this is Peter's go, not a reversible self-serve step.
- **Open tasks (offered to Peter):** the Wikimedia £20 donation is **NOT done** (real payment → prepare-and-surface, Peter pays); the Porsche warranty write-up to **re-deliver** — each as one clean Marie turn (deliver-first). Smaller: browser fill robustness on the WMF gateway — see [P6-117] for the corrected root cause.
- **UPDATE — fundamental review commissioned.** Peter (4-Jul): "we keep hitting memory/context/bloating/compaction/cost over ~10 sessions — it's the crux of all failures AND high cost; stop patching a fundamentally flawed system, review core principles + best practice (our KB + latest sources), refactor, come up with something that finally works." Agreed. Wrote **`_session-docs/MEMORY-CONTEXT-ARCHITECTURE-REVIEW.md`** (committed `d5f6541`) — first-principles diagnosis: **the root flaw is the absence of a retrieval layer** (everything is injected wholesale or dumped to flat append-only logs; the only knob is inject-more↔inject-less), a **positive-feedback loop** (context→compaction→flush-append→bigger files→bigger injection), and the **three-memory-types conflation** (working/episodic/semantic all handled as "write flat file + inject it"). Six redesign principles + a dedicated-session plan with a **measurable acceptance gate** (v2 must demonstrably kill each past incident). **This becomes the LEAD of 6c.21** ([P6-116] behavioural rules are explicitly labelled coping-not-fix).
- **— DONE 6c.35 (RATIONALE-rotation executed):** `workspace-pa/MEMORY.md` had drifted to **6467 chars — over the 5909 hard cap** (tail-truncates → newest Trust-critical rules at risk; the P6-146 screenshot-rule expansion pushed it over, and the 07-13 rotation had logged detail to RATIONALE without trimming MEMORY.md). Rotated the coldest **fully-RATIONALE-backed** blocks (Timezones 5-rule detail, Booking, Competence, the Learnings-promotion meta-rule) to triggers-plus-pointers + tightened verbose bullets in place (no directive dropped, every P-code preserved). **`4e5409f74bf9`→`7f8cb02ea6a4`/5556 chars** (353 headroom under the cap); rotated detail captured in `reference/MEMORY-RATIONALE.md` (`a3da7003224b`→`83b43c957cb5`) under a dated `## Rotated 2026-07-15` log. Silent-truncation bug closed with durable headroom. (The deeper retrieval-layer refactor remains the separate memory-architecture item.)

### P6-117 — 6c.20→21: the "card issue" ROOT-CAUSED — payment-form automation reliability (hidden custom radios + SPA handlers), a substrate distinct from memory; Wikimedia + test-cred closed
**Type:** diagnosis + loop-closure · **Status:** diagnosed; two loops closed manually by Peter; the automation track is deferred. **Trigger:** Peter: "fix the card issue so we can test Wikimedia and close it off + delete the test cred" (in the GUI).
- **Context check (Peter: "you are in GUI, always check before asking"):** verified empirically — `SSH_CONNECTION` empty, `launchctl managername = Aqua`, gui/502 reachable ⇒ I'm in the GUI session; GUI-bound ops (gateway restart, LaunchAgents) ARE available to me. Corrected my prior SSH assumption. **Lesson: probe the execution context, don't assume it.**
- **Root cause (host-reproduced, no charge):** drove the real WMF `donate.wikimedia.org` £20 one-off flow myself. The amount options are **custom-styled radios whose real `<input>`s are hidden ("not visible")**, and the flow is **SPA-handler driven**. So: `click <ref>` fails "Element eN not found or not visible" **even on a snapshot taken one command earlier** (reproduced Marie's exact `e8/e9` error); the `evaluate` label-click *registers* but **does not advance** the SPA to the `payments.wikimedia.org` gateway. So [P6-116]'s "aria snapshot unsupported" read was incomplete — the **ai snapshot works fine** here; the real walls are **hidden inputs + framework click-handlers**. This is a **second flawed substrate, separate from memory**: browser automation on complex payment SPAs (stale/hidden refs + SPA handlers) — a cousin of the Trust-Payments OOPIF case ([P6-111]).
- **Discipline held:** 2 attempts then **stopped** (1–2-tries-then-hand-back, [P6-51/P6-102]) — did NOT grind a payment form; left Chrome clean on the £20 page for Peter.
- **Loops CLOSED (Peter, manually, in the GUI):** the **Wikimedia £20 one-off donation is DONE**; the **throwaway test item `agm4bg3fupvstogchryz75uwri` is DELETED** from Agent-Provisioned (`op item delete` stays deny-listed for me — Peter ran it). Both [P6-115]/[P6-116] open tasks now closed.
- **Deferred (own track, not the memory session):** robust payment-form automation. **Honest v1 posture on hard gateways (Wikimedia / Trust-Payments / Stripe): Marie drives to the page + surfaces the last mile; Peter completes the card+click** — do not claim full auto-fill on arbitrary SPAs. Full auto is a real engineering track → PRE-COS-BACKLOG.

### P6-118 — 6c.21: Memory/Context Architecture v2 designed — the review's two premises corrected empirically; OpenClaw already ships the retrieval stack (it's switched OFF); design + staged migration + measurable gate delivered
**Type:** foundational design + KB/empirical correction + external-best-practice research · **6c.21 (GUI/Aqua, D20 satisfied — `SSH_CONNECTION` empty, `managername=Aqua`)** · **Status:** DESIGN COMPLETE; migration + interim stabiliser **Peter-gated** (need a sanctioned `openclaw.json` path + GUI restart — not applied this session). **openclaw.json UNCHANGED all session** (`da191cf1920d`/10099B, A-7 clean live==last-good, 600/staff). The LEAD of the session per [P6-116]'s commissioned review.

**Deliverable:** `_session-docs/MEMORY-ARCHITECTURE-v2.md` (`913edfdf6a79`/31574B, 11 sections) — the v2 design doc: six principles → concrete OpenClaw wiring; a validation matrix (each past incident → the v2 mechanism that kills it); a 7-step staged/measured migration under F17/P6-24; a measurable acceptance gate; the interim stabiliser; and the decisions surfaced to Peter.

**Two premises of `MEMORY-CONTEXT-ARCHITECTURE-REVIEW.md` corrected empirically (A-12) — the reframe:**
1. **"No retrieval layer" is wrong about the *platform*, right about the *deployment*.** OpenClaw 2026.4.22 natively implements hybrid embedding+FTS retrieval (`memory_search`/`memory_get`), the working/episodic/semantic split (session / `memory/YYYY-MM-DD.md` / `MEMORY.md`), promotion + REM **dreaming** consolidation, recency decay, and an idempotent pre-compaction flush. **All of it is dormant here:** `openclaw memory status` → `Indexed: 0/34 files · 0 chunks` (pa), `0/31` (pro); `Recall store: 0 entries · 0 promoted`; `Dreaming: off`. `memorySearch.enabled=true` but the index was **never built** → `memory_search` returns nothing → agents run 100% wholesale injection with zero retrieval. So v2 is mostly **activation + correct wiring + file restructuring of machinery we already own**, not net-new engineering — a far stronger, cheaper, more reversible "something that finally works."
2. **The review's config-key names don't exist in this build.** `contextLimits.toolResultMaxChars` / `compaction.memoryFlush` / `params.cacheRetention` / `imageMaxDimensionPx` are all nested under **`agents.defaults.*`** (e.g. `agents.defaults.contextLimits.toolResultMaxChars`) — which is why every prior `config get` on the assumed names returned "not found". The real surface was enumerated secret-free via `openclaw config schema`/`get` (the sanctioned read path — `openclaw.json` itself stays deny-Read). Full table in the doc §3.

**Empirical findings this session (all inspection-only, zero billed turns):**
- Real live values: `bootstrapTotalMaxChars=110000` (the "slider": 60→75→110K across [P6-36]/[P6-97]/[P6-98]); `bootstrapMaxChars=30000`; `contextTokens=120000`; `memoryFlush.enabled=true`; `memorySearch.enabled=true`; `dreaming`/`temporalDecay`/`toolResultMaxChars` all at default (off/unset).
- **Raw bootstrap truncation is currently held** (injected set = 8 files ≈ 53K chars per [P6-98]; PLAYBOOK/DECISIONS/USER-CONTEXT/TASKS are reference-only, not injected) — but via the slider, which v2 removes the dependence on.
- **The flush duplication is real and worse than reported:** `memory/2026-07-03.md` (105KB/894 lines) has section headings duplicated **9×**; 07-04 ×3 — the memoryFlush re-append positive-feedback loop, empirically.
- **Empty-index leading cause:** `provider=openai`, no `models.embeddings.openai.apiKey` resolves, and gateway logs show `acpx runtime ready` repeatedly but **zero** reindex/embedding lines → the OpenAI *embedding* key is likely unwired, `sync.onSessionStart` failing silently. Fix at migration: wire it **or** switch to a local GGUF embedder (preferable for a private personal assistant — no external key/spend/dependency).

**External best-practice research (done properly — two primary-sourced tracks, cited in-doc §2):**
- *Anthropic/vendor:* two-tier index+on-demand (Claude Code's own `MEMORY.md` model); cache economics (read 0.1× vs write 1.25×/2×; order prefix stable→volatile — Marie's 2h idle > 5-min TTL is why she re-caches every turn); context-editing (−84% tokens) + compaction + memory role-split; "ASSUME INTERRUPTION" checkpoint discipline; 25K tool-result caps.
- *Academic/industry:* CoALA **four**-store split (working/episodic/semantic/**procedural** — we conflate the 4th); MemGPT/Letta pin-core + page-the-rest + **save-then-evict handshake** (never silent truncation); Generative Agents **recency+importance+relevance** scoring + reflection-with-citations; Mem0/LangMem **idempotent ADD/UPDATE/DELETE/NOOP reconciliation** (the exact fix for the 9× dup); Zep supersession-over-deletion; structured-running-state over freeform-prose as the compaction target.
- **Convergence:** every credible mechanism maps 1:1 to an OpenClaw feature that is off/unset here. The design rests on the agreed *mechanisms*, not on the (mutually-contested, self-reported) cross-vendor benchmarks.

**The v2 design (doc §4–§8):** P1 retrieval-over-injection (small frozen always-on core ≤~30K + turn the index ON + temporalDecay/mmr); P2 four-store separation; P3 tool-result hygiene at source (the caps); P4 compaction-as-safe-checkpoint (deliver-before-compact + idempotent structured-state flush + cheap flush model + keepRecentTokens/identifierPolicy/truncateAfterCompaction); P5 cost-structural (cache-stable prefix, `continuation-skip`, `cacheRetention:long`); P6 observability (a memory-health canary: per-turn tokens, compaction/hour, truncation/day, daily-file dup count, index freshness, cache read:write ratio). Validation matrix maps every [P6-93/97/98/102/103/108/115/116] incident to its killing mechanism. Migration is 7 staged, measured, reversible steps.

**Decisions surfaced to Peter (doc §9) — the gating unblock is #1:** (1) a **sanctioned `openclaw.json` read/edit path** for the config steps (the auto-mode classifier blocks even reading it → can't self-serve the staged F17 edits); (2) GUI restart windows (D20) to measure each lever cleanly; (3) cheap flush/dreaming model (local Ollama vs Sonnet); (4) embedding provider (wire OpenAI embedding key vs local GGUF); (5) small measurement-turn authorisation (cheapest model, [P6-51]). Nothing mutated pending these — the [P6-116] coping rules remain the interim harm-reduction. **Payment-form automation ([P6-111]/[P6-117]) is explicitly a separate track, untouched.**

**UPDATE (same session — Peter: "trust your judgement… make sure the unimplemented research is available to Andreas"). Migration Step 1 SHIPPED + F26-verified; two premises corrected; Andreas inheritance wired.**
- **Retrieval turned ON — the single highest-value, reversible, no-restart step, done + verified.** Provider was ready all along (`memory status --deep`: `Embeddings/Vector/FTS: ready`) — the earlier "embedding key unwired" hypothesis was WRONG (the empty index was simply never built; the "no probe output" was a macOS `timeout`-not-installed artefact, not evidence). `openclaw memory index --force` built **pa 34/34 files·216 chunks, pro 31/31·36 chunks (`Dirty: no`)** — plus the 7 dormant agents. **F26-by-inspection (zero billed turns):** the query "Porsche windscreen warranty write-up" — which returned **`count:0`** on the [P6-116] failure day, causing Marie to rebuild from scratch → lost to compaction → Peter got nothing — now returns the Porsche memory at **0.667 relevance**. The [P6-116] rebuild-from-scratch mechanism is killed at the retrieval layer. `sync.watch`/`onSessionStart` (default true) keep it fresh; the sqlite store persists across restarts. Reversible (clear the index).
- **Premise correction #2 (A-12, from the pinned dist):** `contextLimits.toolResultMaxChars` default = **16000** (`?? 16e3`), i.e. **already tight** — the review's/opener's "single biggest lever … behind the 1.5 M-token turns" is **false**. A 1.5 M-token turn is cumulative session + cache-read of the un-reset `:telegram:direct` history (excluded from the daily freshstart), not one un-capped tool result. The interim stabiliser is therefore **retrieval (done)**, not lowering that cap (which would risk truncating browser snapshots). pa/pro carry **no** per-agent `contextLimits`/`compaction` overrides → `agents.defaults` is authoritative (P6-24 clean). **1. Retrieval-impact check (free, inspection) — inconclusive BY DESIGN, not by omission.** Runtime since the 6c.21 flip was trivial (quiet Sunday: one morning digest + three "inbox clear" beats), so the [P6-116] pattern had no chance to recur *or* be prevented, and `memory_search` was not organically triggered (no turn needed recall — 0 invocations post-flip, matches were tool *definitions*). **2. Daily-file dedup — SHIPPED, provably information-preserving (reversible, backup-first, no restart, no config).** 6c.21 deferred this as "mutation-risk on live memory"; **6c.22 removed that risk empirically first:** the 9× duplication is the non-idempotent flush re-appending the *same running-summary block byte-identically* (measured: 9 occurrences, **1 unique body** each — not a growing/lossy re-summary). So exact-block dedup (split on `## `, keep first occurrence of each unique (heading,body), preserve preamble + perms) is loss-free. Hard invariant enforced: `set(unique blocks)` identical before/after → abort otherwise. Applied to pa 07-02/03/04: **117 duplicate blocks removed, ~183 KB → ~86 KB**, idempotent (re-run = no-op), 0600 preserved, full backup at `_backups-6c22-memory-dedup/`. Re-indexed: **pa 216 → 121 chunks**, `Dirty: no`; Porsche recall reconfirmed at **0.590** (`memory/2026-07-04.md:44-51`). pro was already clean (0 dups). *Operational finding:* a corpus mutation marks the index `Dirty` via `sync.watch`; the **first** search after ran against a mid-rebuild index and returned "No matches" — a second `index` cleared it. **Confirm `Dirty: no` before trusting recall after any mutation** (now a canary metric). *Also learned:* 07-03's "write-up completed" note has **no inline body** — the actual write-up was compaction-lost ([P6-116]); retrieval recalls the *context* but the deliverable must be *regenerated* (→ Porsche re-deliver stays a real task).

**3. Log-only by default (`state/memory-health/daily.log`); Telegram ALARM to Peter only on threshold breach (`ALARM_TELEGRAM=1`) — quiet unless a regression (no-substance-no-message). Wired to `ai.openclaw.memory-health.plist` (daily 23:55, `RunAtLoad`, bootstrapped gui/502). **4. THE NEW FOUNDATIONAL FINDING — two distinct context-loss mechanisms, quantified (A-12, from `model.completed.data`).** The trajectory carries `truncated`, `compactionCount`, `originalBytes`/`limitBytes`, `usage`, `promptCache` natively. Measured over the recent corpus (1001 turns):
  - **Per-turn total tokens: median 392 K, p95 3.76 M, max 16.4 M** (vs §8 gate proposal median <60 K / p95 <200 K → **~6.5× / ~19× over**). Per-day: pa 07-03 median 251 K, **p95 3.88 M, max 8.2 M, 51 compactions**; 07-04 p95 2.74 M, 7 compactions.
  - **`truncated:True` on 677/1001 turns (68%), and `truncated` ⟺ `originalBytes > limitBytes` exactly (677=677=677).** `limitBytes` is a constant **262144 = 256 KB byte cap** on the assembled prompt — **distinct from token-budget compaction** (`compactionCount` is `None` on truncated turns). [P6-98] fixed bootstrap-*file* injection truncation; this whole-prompt **byte-cap truncation was never measured** and is the dominant silent context-loss mode.
  - **631 of the 677 truncations (93%) live in TWO un-reset long-lived sessions:** pa `14b920c0` **490 turns / 454 truncated / 6-day span** (Jun 15–21), pro `a34324aa` **177 turns / 131 truncated / ~26-day span** (Jun 6–Jul 2). These are the "un-reset `:telegram:direct` session" the opener names (item 4) — **excluded from the daily freshstart**, confirmed with hard numbers. The tool-heavy July sessions fail differently — **token-budget compaction** (the [P6-116] Porsche session `96869d34`: 46 compactions, max 8.2 M tok).
  - **`promptCache.retention = "short"`** on every turn → confirms Fault D (5-min TTL vs 2 h heartbeat re-caches every turn; one turn cacheRead 4.0 M).
  - *Diagnosis:* **long-lived sessions → 256 KB byte-cap truncation → fix = periodic structured checkpoint/reset of that session (opener item 4, [P6-93]/[P6-95] continuity-preserving)**; **tool-heavy sessions → token compaction → fix = P3 tool-result/media caps + P4 keepRecentTokens checkpoint.** Two causes, two fixes — do not conflate.

### P6-121 — 6c.24: intra-day `:main`-bloat auto-reset net — the watchdog (fires at 250K) now archives-first `session-freshstart --force --agent <id>` on a `:main` per-turn breach, guarded against interrupting a live human chat
**Type:** reversible build (session-management; no config, no plist, no restart, no billed turn) · **6c.24 (GUI/Aqua, D20 satisfied — `SSH_CONNECTION` empty, `gui/502` reachable, `managername` console = openclaw)** · **Status:** BUILT + DRYRUN-verified end-to-end through the real script; **LIVE on the next 15-min watchdog tick** (interpreter re-reads the script file at each exec — a script-content change needs no `bootout`/`bootstrap`, unlike a plist change). The actual non-dryrun reset+restart path was **deliberately NOT fired** this session (it restarts the live gateway — irreversible-class; it is the SAME mechanism as the proven-live 06:55 freshstart job, invoked with the new `--agent` flag whose selection was separately verified).

**The gap it closes ([P6-120] item-4 residue):** the 06:55 `session-freshstart` LaunchAgent bounds **overnight** `:main` accretion, but a single heavy browser turn ballooned pa:main **0 → 1.43M mid-afternoon** (6c.22 smoke turn) — a once-daily reset can't bound *intra-day* bloat. The `heartbeat-watchdog` already **detected** context bloat ≥250K every 15m (section C, `CONTEXT_BLOAT_TOKENS`) but only **alerted** Peter; it never acted. 6c.24 wires the detector to the self-heal.

**What shipped (two host scripts, git-tracked, fully reversible):**
1. **`session-freshstart.sh` — added `--agent <id>` selector** (arg parse converted `for a in "$@"` → `while (( $# ))` shift-loop; accepts `--agent pa` and `--agent=pa`; validates ∈{pa,pro}). Restricts the reset loop to one agent so a single-agent breach doesn't blow away the healthy agent's `:main`. **Backward-compatible: no `--agent` → both agents** (the 06:55 job's ProgramArguments pass no args → unchanged). `fc75bc0d5133`/6009B → **`55020ef7acd6`/6637B**.
2. **`heartbeat-watchdog.sh` — new section (D) `:main` auto-reset + `run_reset()` dispatch.** Python section (D) reads each agent's `agent:<id>:main` and emits `RESET|<agent>|<inputTokens>` iff: (a) **`inputTokens` ≥ `WATCHDOG_RESET_TOKENS` (250K)** — gated on **inputTokens (the recurring per-turn window cost), NOT totalTokens** (cumulative across the day's beats → would over-trigger; the heavy turn inflates inputTokens, which every subsequent beat re-pays); (b) `:main` is the **live** background session (updatedAt < 6h); (c) **no human chat is active** — any `:telegram:direct:*` touched within `WATCHDOG_HUMAN_ACTIVE_MIN` (10m) DEFERS the reset (a bloated background session can wait 15m; restarting the gateway under Peter mid-conversation cannot be undone). The zsh `run_reset()` then runs `session-freshstart.sh --force --agent <id>`, throttled by a **per-agent epoch sentinel** `logs/heartbeat-watchdog.reset-<agent>.state` (`WATCHDOG_RESET_COOLDOWN_MIN`=90; mirrors the existing `$STATEF` restart-cooldown idiom) — records the cooldown **only on confirmed success** (`grep 'reset applied'`), so an in-flight skip retries next cycle. At most **one reset per cycle** (`did_reset` guard) and the cycle **skips its own liveness/stall check** after a reset (avoids a double-restart on the transiently-stale post-restart beat). Dispatch switched pipe→here-string so `did_reset` propagates (zsh already runs the last pipeline stage in the current shell — the here-string is just cleaner/option-independent; the original "pipe = subshell in zsh" reasoning was **wrong**, empirically corrected in-session). Added `WATCHDOG_SESSIONS_PA/PRO` env overrides (default → real store) for offline fixture tests. `2e93b6c40910`/14313B → **`183896a33dd2`/20438B**.

**F26 verification — the whole decision + selection + cooldown exercised through the real scripts under `WATCHDOG_DRYRUN=1` (no send/restart/reset), fixtures for the store:** ① `--agent` selection: `--dry-run --agent pa` → pa only; `--dry-run` → both (pro correctly SKIPPED in-flight); `--agent bogus` → validation error exit 2. ② section (D): **BREACH** (300K, human idle 3h) → `RESET` emitted → `[DRYRUN] would reset pa via session-freshstart --force --agent pa`; **HUMAN-ACTIVE** (300K, human 5m) → `reset deferred … a human chat is active` (the key safety guard); **STALE `:main`** (300K, 8h) → silent; **BELOW** (7 tok) → silent. ③ cooldown: sentinel 30m → `within reset-cooldown — skip`; 120m → proceeds. ④ **full real-store DRYRUN**: clean `exit 0`, healthy live `:main` (inputTokens 7) → nothing triggered (true-negative). `zsh -n` clean on both. The one untested arc — an actual reset firing the gateway restart — is the already-live 06:55 mechanism + the verified `--agent` selection; not re-fired here to avoid a live-session interrupt.

**Tunables (env, all default to production values):** `WATCHDOG_RESET_TOKENS`=250000, `WATCHDOG_RESET_COOLDOWN_MIN`=90, `WATCHDOG_HUMAN_ACTIVE_MIN`=10; test: `WATCHDOG_DRYRUN`, `WATCHDOG_SESSIONS_PA/PRO`. **openclaw.json UNCHANGED this session** (`eb08cfa7d7b6`/10654B per 6c.23 close — no config edit made; A-7 unbroken).

### P6-134 — 6c.29 (Peter: "Marie never sent the CeFoLiAc follow-up she claims"): NOT a fabrication — real send, silent cc-drop tool bug; gmail_helper `--to/--cc` last-wins fixed + recipient-verify brief note
**Type:** honesty-incident investigation (fabrication hypothesis REFUTED) + tool bug fix + brief note · **6c.29** · billed £0 (host-side trajectory forensics + dry-run; no agent turns).
- **★ Verdict: the send is REAL — fabrication hypothesis refuted on evidence.** Peter reported the CeFoLiAc French follow-up (French lessons for Leo, Saint-Jean-Cap-Ferrat) missing from his inbox/spam, suspected invention. Marie's OWN 12:41 memory note had self-accused ("## 12:41 — POSSIBLE TENTH FABRICATION … no `<function_calls>` block … msgId invented"). **Both wrong.** Trajectory `1e128728` holds two genuine `role=toolResult` records: (a) an `exec` of `gmail_helper.py … send-draft --id r1021221674815158398` → `{"messageId":"19f46a0b5109dfea","threadId":"19f3e3a9f9051126","sent":true}`; (b) a later verification `list` finding it in **SENT** (from Marie <marie@fedchenkov.com>, correct subject/snippet). The 12:41 self-accusation was a **flush-turn context-truncation false-alarm** (the tool result wasn't in the compacted view); the 12:42 mirror-rule reversal ([P6-103]) was **correct** — it stopped Marie dis-claiming real work. **The mirror rule worked exactly as intended** (contrast [P6-128]).
- **★ Why Peter couldn't see it — silent cc-drop tool bug.** Marie's draft call was `draft --to info@cefoliac.com --cc pfedchen@gmail.com --cc olga.gladkova@bk.ru` (Peter named first). `gmail_helper.py`'s `draft`/`send` defined `--cc`/`--to` **single-valued** (no `action="append"`, unlike `modify`'s `--add/--remove`), and `_build_message` sets `msg["Cc"] = a.cc` (one string) → argparse keeps only the **last** repeated flag → Cc collapsed to Olga-only; **Peter silently dropped**. Her "cc'd to you" was honest intent defeated by the tool. (The `send` path worked when she used one comma-separated `--cc` — inconsistent usage exposed the latent bug.) Peter confirmed live: "I can see the email in her sent — she only copied Olga and skipped me."
- **★ Fix (Peter chose tool-fix + brief note):** `--to`/`--cc` on both `draft` and `send` → `action="append"`, plus a post-parse normaliser comma-joining the list back to a string (downstream stays string-typed; repeated-flag AND comma-sep both work; single-recipient unaffected). Dry-run proven: two `--cc` → `"cc":"pfedchen@gmail.com,olga.gladkova@bk.ru"`. Deployed to the **bind source** `agent-creds/gmail_helper.py` (= container `/opt/gmail_helper.py`, ro bind → live, no restart; same source serves Charlotte): `f2ed9ce6caaa`/13190B → **`f14489444597`/13596B** (agent-tools mirror synced identical). Backup `scripts/gmail_helper.py.pre-6c29-p6134`. **Brief note** (AGENTS.md L21): "A send's to/cc I report from its result, not the flags I passed ([P6-134])." SHA `aa9821629893`/16597B → **`8ab05e5f7838`/16673B** (1B under the 16674B proven-safe ceiling; both P6-133+P6-134 notes present).
- **Residual:** F26 end-to-end (a real multi-cc send landing both recipients) verifies organically on Marie's next such send — not billed (Peter declined a CeFoLiAc re-send; the vendor already has the correct threaded copy). Marie's in-flight memory lesson had **mis-diagnosed** the cause as "forgot to cc / wrong mailbox"; the real cause is this tool bug — now closed. **docker exec** into the pa sandbox was **denied** mid-session (verified recipients from the trajectory instead — did not route around).

### P6-136 — 6c.30: T5 account-create autonomy uplift — the "L1 refusal" is brief-policy + model-reticence (NOT a runtime guard); "gate at value" enabled + Sonnet-validated; live E2E blocked on an unbuilt host credential-fill → Andreas §C

Only the Tier-2 `browser_helper.py` `fill-and-shot` verbs carry a **script-level** guard — `--fill` refuses password/payment selectors, `--click` refuses commit buttons — but account tasks use Tier-1. That script guard is why Marie's older memory (2-Jul) says "my tools refuse password+submit".)*
- **★ Autonomy decision (Peter, AskUserQuestion): "gate at value."** Marie **creates + saves accounts autonomously** for **free/reversible** signups; she surfaces-before-submit **only** at genuine choke-points — **(a)** any payment/pay-click (never auto-charge), **(b)** a signup demanding **government-ID/strong-identity proof or that links a financial account**, **(c)** **consequential legal T&Cs**. Pay-click stays gated regardless. A choke-point rule, **not** a category allowlist (matches [[security-design-philosophy]] gate-value-at-the-card + [[agent-payments-autonomy-model]]). - **★ Behavioural validation — PASS (Sonnet, production-class).** `openclaw infer model run --gateway --model anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-6` (real gateway, not `--local` embedded) fed the two edited brief rules + a 4-scenario probe → **all four gate decisions correct**: recipe-newsletter (name+email) = **DO**; England-Golf £47 = **SURFACE** (payment); NHS portal (NHS-number + photo-ID) = **SURFACE** (strong-identity); free Goodreads (email-verify) = **DO** (verification is routine, not a gate). - **★ Live E2E BLOCKED on an unbuilt host credential-fill (create-side twin of the T4 card gap) — stopped before any spend.** `generate` mode requires the **host** to fill the op-generated password into the signup form ("the model never sees it") — but that host-fill **is not implemented**: `pay-fill.sh` is **card-only** (hardcoded ccnum/cvv/expiry/cardholder by card-UUID); `cred-save*.sh` only **stores** (receipt note literally `"op_ref for a later host fill"` — intent, no code); a repo-wide grep finds **no `cred-fill`/password-into-form handoff**. So a config-swap + billed browser turn would have **failed at the password step on a known gap** → not run (cost discipline [P6-51]; [[no-unauthorized-test-spend]]). This is the same class as the [P6-135] hosted-field card-fill → **[P6-130] Andreas §C** (host secret → cross-site form fill).

This Claude-Code session is **F21-blocked** from `jq`/`mv`/`cp` on `openclaw.json` (shasum is allowed; `config get`/`config set` are not path-blocked) → a byte-safe swap+revert would be **Peter-run via `!`** (revert = restore from `openclaw.json.last-good`). Peter chose "swap + run now", but the cred-fill gap made the turn moot → **no swap performed**.

### P6-142 — 6c.32: adversarial pre-push self-audit of the Andreas build (Peter-requested) — 2 reviewers (code + v7 §S11/§SR-1 design) surfaced real robustness bugs + design under-specification; cheap correctness bugs FIXED & re-tested (20/20), genuine design decisions FLAGGED for 6d live-wiring. v7 self-audit answered: record additively, defer the v7 reconcile to Andreas.
**Type:** adversarial review + remediation (Peter: "double-check you haven't forgotten or misimplemented anything… run the [v7] self-audit… or defer to Andreas?") · **6c.32** · £0 (two Claude-Code review subagents = my own operation; all a2a-watch repros in a scratch `A2A_ROOT`, dryrun, no dispatch/spend). **openclaw.json UNCHANGED** (`3267edd8b6aa`/10489B, A-7 clean).
- **★ Method.** Before the surfaced `git push`, ran two parallel adversarial reviewers + my own direct checks. Direct checks **clean**: all 9 files referenced by Andreas's AGENTS.md resolve; **no restricted-data leak** (Andreas correctly lacks `USER-CONTEXT-RESTRICTED.md`); no stale filenames; every sha in the closure table matched disk.
- **★ Verdict (both reviewers):** the build is **structurally faithful** to v7 — all five S11 layers + all four SR-1 checks correctly wired. The problems are (a) real **robustness bugs** in the code and (b) genuine **under-specification in v7 §S11** the code faithfully inherited. **Safe to push as an inert foundation** (quadruple-guard holds) **once the cheap bugs are fixed** — several bite the very first 6d "dryrun over real traffic" step.
- **★ FIXED now (fix-now; re-tested — a2a-watch 20/20, carry-chain all-green). `a2a-watch.py` `a8b0c2f68aed`→`f3460ae17105`/19660B; `carry-chain-audit.py` `d71982c77be9`→`375f8e9dc1e9`/15102B:**
  - **#1 BLOCKER — a malformed agent request wedged the whole mailbox.** A valid-JSON-but-hostile request (non-dict body / non-list `path` → `TypeError` on `to in path` / unhashable `conversation_id`) threw an *uncaught* exception, aborting the poll; the poison file stayed in `pending/` → crash-loop every 60s + blocked everything behind it — defeating the "un-jammable hard mechanism". **Fix:** per-request `try/except` (last-resort quarantine → drop+move, never wedge) + type-guards (require dict body, list `path`, non-empty-str key fields). Proven: poison drops, the good request behind it still processes, `pending/` left empty.
  - **#2 BLOCKER-for-live — counters not crash-durable + move-after-dispatch double-bill.** `save_counters` ran once post-loop (a mid-poll crash lost the whole poll's accounting) and `move_processed` ran *after* `dispatch` (a kill between → re-dispatch → double-billed). **Fix:** save counters per-request; **claim-before-dispatch** (move out of `pending/` before the billed turn).
  - **#3 — dryrun wrote a real `HALT`.** 30 would-allows drove `fleet_billed`→ceiling and `trip_halt()` wrote a live kill-switch during an observe-only run. **Fix:** `trip_halt` LIVE-only (dryrun logs a *would-trip*); **per-MODE counter files** (`a2a-counters-<mode>-…`) so dryrun never pollutes the live counter the first enablement step reads.
  - **#5 hop** accepted `true` (`isinstance(True,int)`) and `0`/negative → reject bool + `hop<1`. **#9** missing `message` passed dryrun but `KeyError`'d live → require non-empty message for message-type. **#12** `move`/`write_result` silently overwrote same-basename → collision-safe suffixing. **#13** spawn timestamp list grew unbounded → prune-on-write.
  - **Design #5 — fleet ceiling (30) equalled the hub daily budget (30)** → L3 auto-HALT would trip on a *normal* busy hub day, not as an anomaly backstop. **Fix:** default `A2A_FLEET_DAILY` **30→60** (above the per-agent sum 30+10+10).
  - **#8 model no-op** — `openclaw agent` has **no `--model` flag** on 2026.4.22 (A-12 verified) → dropped the misleading plumbing; `model` is ledger-metadata only (tier = agent config).
  - **SR-1 #11 fail-open** — check 2 returned PASS on a typo'd `--since` ref and passed **vacuously** post-commit with the default `HEAD`. **Fix:** **fail-closed** on a bad/unknown ref; warn on the vacuous-HEAD case; COS-PLAYBOOK §Close-discipline now says invoke `--since <prior-close-ref>`, pre-commit. **SR-1 #10** — carry-diff silently missed **numbered-list** carried items (regex only matched `-`/`*`) → broadened to ordered lists (verified: a numbered dropped item is now flagged NOT-FOUND).
- **⛔ FLAGGED for 6d A2A-wiring (genuine design decisions — NOT fixed; recorded in `shared/a2a/README.md §Open` + PRE-COS-BACKLOG + the 6c.33 opener):**
  - **#4 (the #1 must-resolve-before-live gate) — the L1 cycle-check and the L2 per-ordered-pair budget cannot both be live for a direct reply.** As written (`to in path` → cycle), a normal A→B→A reply is dropped, so the per-pair budget (whose job is "kills ping-pong") is dead in the reply direction; the README's own canonical envelope self-rejected. The deciding piece — the **agent-side envelope constructor** (who mints `conversation_id`, increments `hop`, appends `path`, whether a reply resets it) — is **unspecified in v7 AND unbuilt**; it depends on the chosen **topology** (hub-synchronous `--deliver`-returns vs peer-relay messages). Left provisional: the numeric budgets are the robust primary guard, the cycle-check is belt-and-braces, and the README example is corrected to a valid first-hop. **6d must decide topology + envelope construction before A2A goes live.**
  - **Design #2 — provenance is agent-asserted, host-validated only.** L1 is hard against *accidental* loops (the real 6c.7 threat) but not a mis-constructed envelope. 6d decides: host reconstruct `path`/`hop` from `ledger.jsonl` per `conversation_id` (robust) vs accept the accidental-only threat model + document it.
  - **#7 midnight reset** of conversation-scoped budgets (per-day counter file); **design #4 L3 units** (a turn-count proxy today, not the real £/Console hook); **#13 fanout gameable via `hop` variance** (theoretical with 3 agents). All tuning/wiring items.
- **★ v7 self-audit — Peter's question answered.** The design reviewer confirmed v7 §S11 under-specifies the reply/topology model (the root of #4) and §SR-1 omits the prior-close-ref + the spawn budget + names the wrong docs repo (already [P6-141]). **Recommendation adopted (matches the doc-tier discipline): record findings ADDITIVELY** — this P6-142 + the README `§Open` + PRE-COS-BACKLOG gates + the corrected live briefs — **and do NOT patch the sha-anchored v7 snapshot mid-build.** Rewriting v7 now would break snapshot discipline and risk cementing v1 build choices (repo name, spawn omission, L3 proxy) as design intent; the two load-bearing findings are unresolved *design*, not typos. The v7 §S11/§SR-1 reconcile is **Andreas's first doc-currency milestone job**, where all fold in together. **No build/doc discrepancy created** — the live briefs/README/backlog carry the truth; v7 is flagged, not silently divergent.
- **SHA anchors (remediation):** `a2a-watch.py`→`f3460ae17105`/19660B; `carry-chain-audit.py`→`375f8e9dc1e9`/15102B; `shared/a2a/README.md` `f08b7fa26028`→`ee882782c770`/5191B; `workspace-cos/COS-PLAYBOOK.md` `c05bfb71baa4`→`670b101e00c8`/20474B; AGENTS/TOOLS/HEARTBEAT/SOUL unchanged. openclaw.json UNCHANGED (`3267edd8b6aa`/10489B).
- **★ Net:** the inert foundation is now **robust** — a hostile request can't wedge the mailbox, dryrun can't spend or false-trip a live HALT, and the SR-1 integrity check fails closed. The genuine design gaps are **explicit, gated must-resolve-before-A2A-live items** (not silent). Both reviewers' final verdict: **safe to push.**

### P6-143 — 6c.32 (post-close, Peter: "Marie stopped adding her signature in the last couple of emails"): NOT Marie forgetting, NOT a regression — the signature is bolted to the `send` verb only; her L1 draft→send-draft approve-flow never signs. Fix prepared (sign at draft-time for send-identities); apply = Peter's `!` run (deny-Read helper).
**Type:** investigation + prepared fix · **6c.32 post-close** · £0 (host-side brief/backup/memory inspection; no billed turn; no secret-value read — the live `agent-creds/gmail_helper.py` is deny-Read, diagnosed via the readable `scripts/gmail_helper.py.pre-6c29-p6134` backup + Marie's memory). openclaw.json UNCHANGED (`3267edd8b6aa`/10489B).
- **★ Mechanism.** The canonical signature (P6-103, `Marie / AI personal assistant to Peter Fedchenkov ✨ / marie@fedchenkov.com`) is auto-appended by `gmail_helper._build_message(a, with_from=True)` — Marie writes body only, never hand-types it. **But `with_from=True` is passed by the direct `send` verb ONLY** (`cmd_send`): `cmd_draft` builds with `with_from=False` (**unsigned**), and `cmd_send_draft` POSTs the stored draft by id and **never rebuilds the message** (so it structurally cannot sign).
- **★ Root cause (evidence-backed, [[dont-overassert-researched-conclusions]]).** Marie's L1 prepare-and-surface flow shifted to the **draft workflow** — create a Gmail draft, surface it, and on approval send via **`send-draft`**. Her own 2026-07-10 memory is explicit: "that'll surface when Peter says 'send' and the **send-draft** call fails", plus a "draft-hygiene" note about accumulating draft copies + `send-draft` on approval. Earlier signed emails (e.g. the 7 Jul CeFoLiAc enquiry) used **direct `send`** (auto-signs). So as she moved `send` → `draft`+`send-draft`, the signature silently vanished — and she still believes it auto-appends (memory: "helper auto-appends signature — did NOT hand-type"), so she never flagged it. **Not a regression** — the 6c29 [P6-134] edit only touched `--to/--cc` parsing (unchanged `_build_message`/`cmd_draft`), confirmed against the readable backup. Same "soft mechanism silently fails on the actual workflow" class as [P6-128]/[P6-142].
- **★ Fix (prepared, not yet applied — deny-Read live shared component).** Sign at DRAFT time for send-identities, mirroring exactly what makes a `send` sign: `cmd_draft` → `msg = _build_message(a, with_from=(getattr(a, "account", None) in SEND_IDENTITIES))`. Signs `marie@` drafts (so `send-draft` sends them signed); leaves drafts-as-Peter (`pfedchen@`, not a send-identity) unsigned — correct on both. Self-verifying **abort-safe idempotent** apply script `scripts/apply-6c33-sig-on-draft.py` (backs up → `scripts/gmail_helper.py.pre-6c33-sig`; prints SEND_IDENTITIES scope so we confirm only marie@ is affected; aborts untouched if the `cmd_draft` line isn't found exactly once; sha before/after). **Apply = Peter's `!` run** (`agent-creds/**` is deny-listed for my Bash; I never route around it). Live immediately via the ro bind, no restart (per [P6-134]).
- **★ APPLIED (Peter, 6c.32 post-close) — code-level verified.** The `scripts/gmail_helper.py.pre-6c33-sig` backup exists (so the script passed its abort gates and patched), its pre-patch sha `f14489444597`/13596B **matches the live helper sha exactly** (right file, the bind source), and the scope gate confirmed `SEND_IDENTITIES = {"marie@fedchenkov.com"}` (only marie@ affected — no cross-agent interaction). Pre `f14489444597`/13596B → **expected live `5ce4b5ca4ca4`/13646B** (computed from the backup + the exact one-line replacement; cross-check `shasum ~/.openclaw/agent-creds/gmail_helper.py`). **Remaining = the end-to-end F26** (a real marie@ send now carries the signature — will confirm on Marie's next such send) + the agent-tools mirror re-sync (→ 6c.33).
- **★ Open follow-ups (→ 6c.33):** (a) Peter runs the apply script + verify a real marie@ send signs; (b) **re-sync the agent-tools mirror** copy if kept separately from the bind source ([P6-134] noted a mirror); (c) if the live `SEND_IDENTITIES` lists accounts beyond `marie@` that shouldn't carry Marie's (hardcoded) signature, review that pre-existing `send`-path property separately; (d) the offline `draft --dry-run` preview won't show the new signature (it returns before creds load, so `a.account` is unset) — cosmetic, real drafts sign correctly.

### P6-146 — 6c.33: Marie screenshot-delivery F26 = **FAIL**, mechanism pinpointed (agent-turn `MEDIA:~/…` tilde **text** directive, not a structured photo attachment). Advances [P6-144]④; payments/booking-critical → carried to a focused fix.
**Type:** F26 verification (negative) + sharp root-cause · **6c.33** · £0 host-side diagnosis + one billed Sonnet Marie turn (bundled per [P6-144]④).
- **Test.** Flipped `pa` opus→sonnet; Marie asked to screenshot example.com and send it. **Result: FAIL** — no image reached Peter; Marie narrated "example.com… screenshot delivery working" — a **false receipt** ([P6-128] honesty miss).
- **Mechanism (host-log, £0).** The screenshot PNG **WAS created** (`media/browser/a048acc0-…png`, 13:43 — the verb ran), but delivered as a **`MEDIA:~/.openclaw/media/browser/<uuid>.png` text directive with a tilde path** → every telegram send is `sendMessage` (text), **zero `sendPhoto`** → the attachment is stripped, nothing arrives. The channel attaches host-**absolute** structured `mediaUrl`/`--media` (proven by the [P6-144]④ msg-1685 host-side test Peter confirmed) — **not** a `~/…` tilde text line.
- **Advances [P6-144]④.** That entry *isolated* the bug to the agent-turn attachment path (by inference from the host-side `--media` success); **this F26 confirms the agent path fails AND names the mechanism.** Marie's brief belief ("`browser screenshot` verb delivers natively — structured image"; PA-PLAYBOOK §Payments / MEMORY.md, from [P6-103] line-854) is **FALSE on the agent path** — line-854's "delivers fine, dozens of sends" was send-history `mediaUrl`-payload inference, never receipt, now falsified twice.
- **Fix direction (CARRIED — deliberately not rushed at session-end on a payments-critical path).** Make the agent screenshot-reply a **structured absolute-path attachment** (as `message send --media` does), not a `MEDIA:~/…` tilde text line: locate where the tilde originates (browser screenshot verb return / Rich-Output-Protocol reply handling / sandbox helper) and whether it's fixable at config/brief or is dist-level (browser last-mile [P6-130]/Andreas). - **★ 6c.34 — RESOLVED, F26 PASS (dist fix + brief).** Root cause was **deeper than the tilde** (the 6c.33 diagnosis was correct-but-partial). TWO layers: **(1)** the reply-text parser (`parse-*.js isValidMedia` → `hasTraversalOrHomeDirPrefix`) rejects any `MEDIA:` path starting `~`/`..` (a real exfiltration guard) → a `~/…` line degrades to literal text; **(2)** the decisive one — for a **sandboxed** agent the reply-media normalizer (`reply-media-paths.runtime`) routes **all** media (native structured attachment *and* hand-typed) through `resolveSandboxedMediaSource → assertSandboxPath`, which requires the **host path inside the sandbox root** (`workspace-pa`). Tier-1 host-Chrome screenshots save to `~/.openclaw/media/browser/<uuid>.png` (global dir, subdir `"browser"` hardcoded at `server-context` saveMediaBuffer sites) — a **sibling of** the workspace → *"Path escapes sandbox root"* → **dropped for ANY path form**. The managed-global whitelist (`MANAGED_GLOBAL_MEDIA_SUBDIRS={"outbound"}`+`tool-*`) built for exactly this system-media case (a) **omitted `browser`** and (b) was **only consulted in the non-sandbox branch** — so host-side `message send --media` delivered (no sessionKey ⇒ no sandbox branch) but the agent turn never could. ⇒ [P6-103]'s "native delivery" belief was **correct-by-design but broken by the containment drop**, not simply false; and no config/brief/symlink workaround exists (dir not mounted; `assertNoPathAliasEscape` blocks symlinks; output dir hardcoded).
- **Fix (minimal, design-faithful, 2 edits to `reply-media-paths.runtime-DegAVXTm.js`).** (i) add `"browser"` to `MANAGED_GLOBAL_MEDIA_SUBDIRS`; (ii) in `normalizeMediaSource`'s sandbox branch, pass **absolute managed-global** media through `persistLocalReplyMedia` **before** the containment assert. Restores the whitelist's original intent. **Security preserved:** `media/{outbound,browser,tool-*}` are NOT mounted into the agent sandbox (agent can't write there — only the host browser tool does), so no arbitrary-file exfiltration; `/etc/passwd`, `agent-creds/**` still fail `isManagedGlobal` → sandbox resolver → escape-root → dropped; the stage-1 `~`/`..` guard is **untouched**. `cf7231b259ef`→**`6dfbfe762078`**/6847B, `node --check` ✓, backup `.orig-6c34`, idempotent re-appliable `scripts/apply-6c34-screenshot-media-fix.sh` (survives an `openclaw` reinstall — dist patch is lost on reinstall of the 2026.4.22 pin; re-run then). Gateway **restart** required to load (module cached per-process).

### P6-149 — 6c.34 (post-close, Peter): Marie comms/task-discipline audit (14–15 Jul Aviva) — status-cadence + live-chat presence fixes baked.
**Type:** behavioural audit + brief fix · **6c.34** · £0 (trajectory forensics + brief edits); Peter-requested ("bake in improvements before we clear; I'll task Marie back on Aviva soon").
- **Trigger.** Peter: Marie "picks up and drops tasks randomly without notification"; "dropped her chat with Aviva today for no obvious reason"; wants status updates "as one could expect from an assistant."
- **Audit (sessions f568f8e9 14 Jul / 530b1fcc 15 Jul).** The Aviva live chat was lost **three times**: (1) 14 Jul 17:15 agent **Satyam closed the chat** because Marie paused ~2 min to draft an auth email; (2) the glass team went **off-shift → 24-min queue**; (3) 15 Jul she re-entered the chat at 09:04 but her **turn ended and the next heartbeat was 10:57 (~2h)** → "chat session gone, browser navigated away," noticed 2h late and mentioned in passing.
- **Root cause = STRUCTURAL, not flakiness.** A live chat needs **continuous real-time presence**; Marie runs in **discrete turns** (2h heartbeats + on-message). Between turns she isn't running, so any live chat started in a turn dies at the turn boundary. She **diagnosed it herself** ("I'll stay glued this time — the last one dropped because I went quiet") and still couldn't — confirming it's the execution model, not discipline.
- **Comms granularity is INVERTED (Peter's core complaint).** Noise when active (per-click narration — "Let me try the chatbot", "clicking No" — each an auto-sent Telegram msg), silence when it matters (the 2h drop window). Both already violate her AGENTS §Notifications ("no step-narration"; "never silent >10–15 min in flight") — so rules alone weren't biting. Plus **draft-thrashing** (3 auth/claim drafts in ~1h, "ignore the last one") and an **out-of-context** msg (the screenshot-F26 "example.com working" landing mid-Aviva).
- **Baked now (brief-level).** **AGENTS.md** (`3c7144b8b1d1`→`c7d8ece4b5ca`) new **§Working a task** — (a) one "On it" then **checkpoints only**, silent through browser drives; (b) **task-state always announced** (Starting/Parking-until/⚠️blocked-dropped), never end a turn mid-task without a "where I've left it" line; (c) **live chat = one sustained sitting** (stay glued, poll ~20–30s, no side-work, keep the turn alive) **or hand back up front**; drop flagged the moment seen; (d) one clean draft per ask. **PA-PLAYBOOK.md** (`0899a049e0b7`→`09108b6184df`) new **live-chat procedure** (anticipate the identity/auth check *before* entering; queue-handback script; drop-flag script).
- **Residual (capability, NOT fixed now).** The brief keep-alive is behavioural (poll-loop keeps one turn alive) — bounded by turn/step limits + cost; a **true engine-level keep-alive / fast re-wake during an active live task** is a capability item (Andreas/6d). For long queues Marie now hands the decision to Peter rather than dropping. **Before re-tasking Aviva:** it's a live-chat task → expect a continuous billed session once an agent joins (authorise the spend), and have Peter's authorisation-to-discuss ready up front.

### P6-150 — 6c.35: morning-message DE-DUPE resolved → **flip to CoS-consolidated** (Peter) + ★ finding: the designed `shared/daily-digests` handoff is UNREACHABLE from agent sandboxes. Built Phase-1 (reversible, no double/no gap) + a Peter-run turnkey Phase-2 activation. A2A gate-coding deferred (Peter).
**Type:** capability wiring + architecture finding · **6c.35** · £0 (host-side script/brief authoring + DRYRUN); openclaw.json UNTOUCHED (`24715f4045bd`/10748B, A-7 clean). Resolves the [P6-148] carried de-dupe/source-reconciliation task.
- **Problem.** The 6c.34 CoS-briefing plist (`gui/502`, `--send --target 253509519`, **08:00 daily**, first auto-fire 16 Jul) and Marie's **own** curated 08:00 digest (PA-PLAYBOOK §Daily digest) both fire at 08:00 → **two morning messages** to Peter tomorrow. The briefing is a **£0 host raw-memory extract**; Marie's is an **agent-curated decision-aid** — a naive swap would *regress* quality; and the briefing **leads with a 36h calendar**, conflicting with **P10-06** ("don't volunteer calendar; Peter knows his commitments").
- **Immediate de-dupe (reversible, zero-regret, done first).** Added a **send-interlock** mirroring the A2A `shared/a2a/HALT` lever: while `shared/cos/BRIEF-SEND-HOLD` (`5bf8c263207b`) exists, `cos-briefing.py --send` **assembles + logs** the briefing (proves the £0 pipeline daily) but **does NOT send**. Verified: the exact plist command hits the HOLD and suppresses the send. Marie's curated digest stays the sole morning message → **no double tomorrow**, no quality regression, no launchctl/Peter step needed.
- **★★ FINDING — the designed handoff was structurally unreachable.** Both briefs designate `shared/daily-digests/<date>/<id>.md` as the fleet-digest handoff (and it "sat empty" — assumed neglect). Root cause via `docker inspect`: the **`pa` sandbox mounts ONLY `workspace-pa → /workspace`** (same for `pro`) — **`shared/` is NOT mounted**, so a sandboxed agent **cannot write** `shared/daily-digests/…`. The location was never reachable; the empty dir was structural, not neglect. **Correction:** the reachable handoff must live inside the agent's own workspace — **`workspace-<id>/memory/digest-<date>.md`** (agent writes `/workspace/memory/digest-<date>.md`; host reads directly). Applies to any future cross-agent file handoff: route via each agent's workspace + host relay, never a shared/ path the sandboxes can't see.
- **`cos-briefing.py` (`7d98572cb1c3`→`c7cd8b395f88`/9094B).** (1) `digest_section` now reads **primary** `workspace-<id>/memory/digest-<date>.md` **verbatim** (the curated handoff), **fallback** to the raw `memory/<date>.md` section-pick heuristic — both branches unit-tested in isolation. (2) `build_briefing` **reordered** to LEAD with the decision-aid (agent digests + open todos) and **demote** the calendar to a non-leading `📅 Day ahead (for prep):` footer — honours P10-06 while keeping the day-ahead Peter opted into. DRYRUN-verified.
- **Peter's decision (6c.35, AskUserQuestion):** **flip to CoS-consolidated** — retire Marie's direct send; the CoS briefing becomes the single morning message. (He also **deferred A2A** gate-coding to a focused run — see below.)

### P6-151 — 6c.35 (post-close, Peter): can Andreas's heavy "Claude Code work" run on Peter's Claude Max sub instead of the metered API? — **VERIFIED NO; runs on metered API, cost-controlled by model-tiering.** + a cost-lane-follows-autonomy principle for the operating model.
**Type:** cost-architecture decision + feasibility finding · **6c.35 post-close** · £0 (claude-code-guide research, sourced). Feeds v7 PART 7 (cost) + the pending Andreas operating-model section ([P6-150]-adjacent; see [[andreas-north-star-autonomous-operator]]).
- **Ask.** Peter: if Andreas runs big chunks of Claude-Code-shaped operator work, route it through his **Claude Max** subscription (flat-rate) rather than the metered API, if cheaper.
- **Verified NO — three converging reasons.** (1) **Technical:** headless/unattended Claude Code needs an `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`; subscription (Max) auth requires an interactive login/keychain session a background agent lacks (official headless docs) — an unattended Andreas can't cleanly use Max anyway. (2) **Policy/account-risk:** Anthropic steers automated/programmatic use to the API; subscription auth is for interactive personal use, and there's **reporting that third-party harnesses — OpenClaw specifically — were blocked/account-banned for subscription-auth automated workloads** (secondary sources; confirm before relying, but an account ban would take the whole fleet down → weight it). (3) **No arbitrage + self-starvation:** SDK/programmatic runs currently count against the subscription's shared pool (no free lunch) and would **starve Peter's own interactive Claude Code** (shared 5h/weekly caps).
- **DECISION.** Andreas's autonomous/unattended work runs on the **metered API**. Cost is controlled by **model/effort tiering** (Sonnet/Haiku bulk, Opus only where it earns it), the **per-task cost tracker** ([P6-85]/[P6-148]), and volume discipline — **not** auth arbitrage.
- **★ Principle — cost lane follows the autonomy level.** Peter running Claude Code **interactively himself** (these sessions) is legitimately on **Max** already; the same operator work run **unattended via Andreas** must be on the **metered API**. So moving operator work up the autonomy ladder ([P6-49]/north-star) has a real cost consequence — it shifts spend from flat Max onto the meter. This must be an explicit input to the Andreas autonomy-ladder / operating-model design, not discovered later.

### P6-152 — 6c.36: A2A live groundwork — the [P6-145] gates **(a) hub-synchronous inline reply + (b) host-authoritative hop/path** CODED + unit-tested + **production dryrun-bootstrapped** through the real launchd path. Design ratified by Peter at the top of the build. A2A stays INERT.
**Type:** S11 loop/cost-protection hardening (the #1 must-resolve-before-live gate) · **6c.36** · GUI/D20 · £0 (dryrun throughout — no dispatch, no billed turn); openclaw.json UNTOUCHED (`24715f4045bd`/10748B, A-7 clean). Closes [P6-142] #4 (the reply/cycle-topology gate) and #2 (provenance hardening).
- **Ratification (top of build, per the opener).** Presented the [P6-145] recommendation grounded in the actual `a2a-watch.py` (which trusted **agent-supplied** hop/path — an agent could under-report `hop` to evade the TTL). Peter ratified the design **and** the scope (**code both gates + unit tests + dryrun-bootstrap; no live flip**).
- **Gate (a) — HUB-SYNCHRONOUS inline reply.** `dispatch()` now returns a 3-tuple capturing the target's turn output; the reply is written **inline into the *requester's* result receipt** (`{"decision":"dispatched","from":<to>,"reply":…}`). Agents therefore **never mint a reverse `B→A` envelope** — so the L1 cycle check needs no "immediate-reply-exempt" carve-out ([P6-142] #4's open question). Only a genuinely new onward dispatch (A→B, then B→C) is an envelope + burns a hop.
- **Gate (b) — HOST-AUTHORITATIVE hop/path.** New `read_accepted_records()` + `reconstruct_hop_path(conv, from)`: before validate/budget the watcher **rebuilds** `hop`/`path` from `ledger.jsonl` lineage per `conversation_id` (first-reach parent map → `path=[root…from]`, `hop=len(path)`), **overriding** the agent-asserted values, which survive only as logged hints (`hop_claimed`/`path_claimed` + a `hop_spoof` flag). Mode-filtered (`event∈{allow,would-allow} ∧ mode==MODE`) so a dryrun reconstruction never inherits live lineage (mirrors the per-mode counters, [P6-142] #3). **Closes the TTL-under-report spoof.** **Honest residual (documented, accepted):** a fresh `conversation_id` resets reconstruction → the per-agent-daily + fleet-daily caps remain the cross-conversation backstop (unchanged).
- **Verified TWO independent ways, both £0.** (1) `scripts/a2a-watch-test.py` (NEW, `cb2496341265`/10597B) — **20/20 checks**: reconstruction correctness (root/deep/unseen/other-conv/first-reach-stable), TTL-under-report **spoof closure** (claimed `hop=1` over a synthetic depth-4 ledger → DROP `hop-exceeded:4>3`, ledger records `hop_spoof=true`), reverse-envelope **cycle** rejection, fan-in still allowed & bounded by the per-pair budget, and gate-(a) inline reply capture (live mode with `subprocess` **monkeypatched** — no real turn). (2) A **production dryrun-bootstrap** of the staged plist through **real launchd** (`apply-6c36-a2a-dryrun-bootstrap.sh`, NEW `4aecca565e1d`/4311B, Peter-run via `!`): `runs=1`/`exit 0`/empty err; over 3 tagged envelopes on the real mailbox → `cos→pa` would-allow (host hop1); `pa→cos` **DROP** `cycle:cos-in-path` (host hop2, spoof=true — reply-envelope rejected); `pa→pro` would-allow at **host hop2** though the agent claimed hop1 (under-report overridden). The script **self-restores**: HALT lifted only for the ~6s poll window then auto-restored (trap-on-exit, fail-closed), booted out, plist uninstalled.
- **Files.** `scripts/a2a-watch.py` **`f3460ae17105`→`96aa0247e52a`**/24246B (433→512L; header + validate_envelope cycle-comment updated to reflect resolution). `shared/a2a/README.md` →**`c7e32cc09426`**/5844B (L1 note = host-reconstructed; "Open" section: both [P6-142] gates marked ✔resolved; remaining = the agent-side envelope emitter + L3 real-£ units). `a2a-watch-test.py` + `apply-6c36-…sh` new. `shared/a2a/ledger.jsonl` now holds the 3 dryrun-smoke records (mode=dryrun evidence — never pollutes live reconstruction).
- **Resting posture (verified restored).** A2A **INERT**: `shared/a2a/HALT` present (fail-closed), plist **staged-not-loaded** (uninstalled from LaunchAgents, job not loaded), `a2a-watch.py` sha unchanged post-run. sessions_send/sessions_spawn still OFF in openclaw.json.
- **Remaining before live (next A2A run).** The **agent-side envelope emitter** is UNBUILT — no agent writes an `.a2a-outbox` yet; wire the AGENTS.md/TOOLS.md convention (mint `conversation_id` at the hub on the human turn; drop a JSON envelope; **read replies from `results/`, never re-send**), dryrun over **real agent traffic**, THEN (Peter-gated, GUI) flip `A2A_MODE=live` + remove HALT + grant `sessions_send` (hard-gate `sessions_spawn`). Kill lever unchanged: `touch shared/a2a/HALT`.

Reconciles/extends [P6-149]/[P6-129]/[P6-116]/[P6-128]/[P6-118]/[P6-85]. Full routing in `PRE-COS-BACKLOG.md §6c.36 addendum`.
- **★ Read: we've been fixing the wrong layer.** 20+ sessions attacked this; the log itself labels most fixes "band-aid/backstop/coping-not-fix".
