- **★ The 16 Jul Aviva instance (one rich case, all 3 symptoms).** 09:18–10:05 she was excellent (continuous clear checkpoints — [P6-149] works when healthy). Then **10:06→11:14 UTC = 68-min SILENCE** on a live high-stakes task: the Aviva chat dropped ~11:04, she never surfaced it, Peter had to poke *"ok, so we wait or what's the plan?"* before she gave status at 11:15. Cost line 11:21: **222.4k tokens** in the turn (1.85× the 120K cap). Live session confirms: `contextTokens=120000`, `totalTokens=128693`, **3 compactions in a 38-min-old session**, ~$0.99 Opus. Memory file freshly **duplicated** (append-only flush re-wrote the earlier block byte-identical). Her own 11:05 "cadence lesson" ("poll completions → NO_REPLY") is what **suppressed the one poll that mattered** (the drop) — noise-suppression vs proactive-status is an unmanaged conflict and she errs to silence.
- **★ Root causes (structural).** (1) **No persistent execution loop** — trigger-only (message / 2h beat / exec-completion); "stay glued" (poll ~25s) forces either context-flooding exec-chains OR turn-end dormancy; today hit both. (2) **Bloat→compaction-thrash** — the human `telegram:direct` session is a single ever-growing context; live-chat/browser tool-noise dumps straight in → 222K → repeated compactions hit the **60s hardcoded timeout (no config knob, [P6-129])** → the status-firing turn stalls. (3) **Lossy/buggy durability** — compaction drops raw context; survival depends on the flush, which is lossy + duplicating + sometimes skipped; MEMORY.md hard-capped ([P6-116]). Corrections to my initial proposal (empiricism): compaction **already** runs on Sonnet (`compaction.model=sonnet-4-6`, `keepRecentTokens=40000`) — that lever is spent; the 60s timeout has **no knob**.
- **★ Note 5 quantified — latency is bloat, not model.** Andreas `telegram:direct` = **44309 tok / 0 compactions / opus-4-7 / $0.025** vs Marie **128693 / 3 / opus-4-7 / $0.99** (40×). Same model + cap. Andreas is fast only because his session is lean+new; **the gap inverts** (he slows as he accretes) without the aggressive-slice root. No separate fix — closes with that root.
- **★ Directive (1) marie@ monitoring — DONE NOW.** Root cause: read helper hardwired to `/creds/google.json` (Peter's box); brief scoped `marie-send.json` to send-only though its `gmail.modify` scope reads. Fixed surgically (brief headroom verified 59K/110K): HEARTBEAT beat + TOOLS now scan `marie@` every beat via `--creds /creds/marie-send.json list`.
- **Directives routed** (full text in backlog): (2) stale-task/draft cleanup → NOW-spec'd, **one policy Q pending** (delete Marie's own stale drafts in Peter's box vs archive/surface-only — her brief currently says "never delete" in his mailbox); (3) `@fedchenkov` deliverability optimisation → **Andreas** (DNS = propose-not-execute); (4) restaurant/place screenshot preferences store → **deferred, event-gated on Travel** (~early Aug, needs retrieval root); (6) reusable micro-skills log → **NOW-lightweight** (`SKILLS.md` append-on-success + consult) **+ Andreas-robust** (reliable only once production retrieval is live). Not over-complicated at the lightweight tier — recommended.
- **★ Andreas-owned durable roots (the case to prioritise Andreas):** aggressive frozen-core brief slice (§A.4 headline); engine-level live-chat keep-alive + bounded worker-session isolation ([P6-149] residual); production retrieval recall activation ([P6-118]/[P6-137]); hard pulse send-gate ([P6-128]) + per-task model routing ([P6-28]/[P6-144]).
- **Safe now-fixes sequenced (non-Andreas):** memory-flush duplication fix; reset-net retune (`CHAT_RESET_TOKENS` 130K→below the 120K cap + graceful in-conversation reset — paired with the durability fix, not shipped alone); **★ status-SLA + compaction-proof open-loops file** (host watcher forces a status when an active loop goes silent past threshold — converts "never go silent" from failed-prose to host-enforced; design-first per Peter); noise-vs-status bright-line.
- **— DELIVERED 6c.37 → [P6-154]/[P6-155]/[P6-156]/[P6-157]/[P6-158]:** the Marie reliability mitigation batch (Stage-1, structural Andreas-INDEPENDENT harm-reducers) shipped. The four durable roots remain Andreas-owned.

### P6-154 — 6c.37: memory-flush duplication ROOT-CAUSED + fixed — persistent information-preserving dedup tool (applied corpus-wide, ~180KB removed) + daily/intra-day cadence; delta-only flush-prompt root staged (Peter: apply at next restart)
**Type:** reliability root-cause + reversible build (host tool + cadence wiring) + staged config-root · **6c.37 (GUI/D20 satisfied — `SSH_CONNECTION` empty, `gui/502` reachable)** · £0 (host-side; no billed turns, no re-index). openclaw.json **UNCHANGED** (`24715f4045bd`/10748B, A-7 clean). Closes the [P6-153] "memory-flush duplication bug"; reconciles [P6-119]/[P6-120].
- **★ Root cause (confirmed).** The pre-compaction memory FLUSH turn regenerates a *cumulative* running-memory block, and the flush write tool is append-only (dist: `wrapToolMemoryFlushAppendOnlyWrite` → "During memory flush, this tool may only append to <path>"). So on a day with N flushes the early sections get re-appended **byte-identically** N times (2026-07-16 = 3× / 8 dup sections; 07-08 = 24×; 07-10 = 25×). This is exactly the [P6-119] finding — whose one-shot dedup was **applied by hand once and never persisted as a scheduled tool** (only `_backups-6c22-memory-dedup/` survived), so dups re-accreted. The knobs `agents.defaults.compaction.memoryFlush.{prompt,systemPrompt}` exist but are **unset** (dist default has no delta-only constraint).
- **★ Fix — host BACKSTOP (shipped, reversible, £0).** `scripts/memory-dedup.py` (`4f5494c5c27d`/6273B): splits a daily file at every heading, keeps the FIRST occurrence of each byte-identical section, drops later identical copies, preserves preamble/trailing-newline/0600, **hard invariant** (unique-section SET identical before/after → else abort the file), idempotent, backup-first (`_backups-memory-dedup/<runstamp>/`), `--dry-run` default. Verified loss-free on a copy (unique-set 14→14 equal, no invented content, preamble preserved, idempotent). **Applied corpus-wide: 92 duplicate sections removed across pa's 8 daily files (~180KB); pro clean (0).** 0600 preserved, idempotent re-check = 0.
- **Cadence wired (no new plist / no Peter bootstrap):** (a) `scripts/memory-health.py` (`969c99ea31e8`/12671B) — new `autoheal_dedup()` runs the tool `--apply` per agent before measuring (daily 23:55; env `MEMORY_DEDUP_AUTOHEAL=0` disables); (b) `scripts/chat-bloat-reset.sh` — intra-day `--apply` on pa's current-day file at the top of each 900s run (isolated + non-fatal, honours the script's `--dry-run`).
- **★ Fix — ROOT prevention (STAGED, Peter-gated).** `scripts/apply-6c37-memory-flush-prompt.sh` (`9433dce0d192`/3344B): F17 apply/revert of a **delta-only** `agents.defaults.compaction.memoryFlush.prompt` ("append DELTA ONLY … everything before the last flush is already saved … re-emit nothing … if nothing new, write nothing"). jq-logic validated on a synthetic fixture (apply sets key + preserves `enabled`; guard passes = only that key differs; revert restores identically). **Peter's 6c.37 decision: STAGE for the next gateway restart** (don't restart solely for this) — the backstop covers it meanwhile. Takes effect on restart; verify by a real flush then `memory-dedup.py --day <today>` = 0 removable. **Re-index NOT run** (was already Dirty 39/47; production recall ~0 [P6-153 root #3]; leaving it lets the eventual Andreas retrieval-activation index the *smaller* deduped files — cost-discipline).

### P6-155 — 6c.37: reset-net retune — `CHAT_RESET_TOKENS` 130K→90K (below the 120K cap) + graceful pre-restart heads-up; paired with [P6-154] (durability), shipped script-only (no restart)
**Type:** reversible build (script edit) · **6c.37** · £0. openclaw.json untouched. Pairs with [P6-154] per [P6-153] ("leaner reloads only safe once memory captures reliably — don't ship alone"). Closes the [P6-153] reset-net item + 6c.36-carried `CHAT_RESET_TOKENS` nudge.
- **Threshold 130K→90K.** `scripts/chat-bloat-reset.sh` (`3a7bd2f71c15`/6744B) default `RESET_TOKENS=${CHAT_RESET_TOKENS:-90000}` (was 130000). 130K sat **above** the 120K context cap, so a reset was only considered *after* compaction-thrash had begun; 90K fires the archive+reset **before** the stick. Installed plist sets no `EnvironmentVariables` (verified — `PlistBuddy` no `:EnvironmentVariables`), so the script default governs; takes effect next 900s tick, **no reload/restart**. Guards unchanged (bloated AND idle≥20m AND cooldown≥120m; archive-first).
- **Graceful heads-up (default on, kill-switch).** Before the restart, if `CHAT_RESET_NOTIFY=1` (default) and Peter was active within `CHAT_RESET_NOTIFY_GRACE_MIN=90`, a **free** gateway-bot Telegram line ("🧹 Just tidying my notes so I stay quick for you — back in a moment") — warm, no technical detail (agent-comms-prefs), never a billed turn. Reset fires only while idle (age≥20m) so this is a courtesy, not mid-conversation. Peter forewarned at the surface; `CHAT_RESET_NOTIFY=0` disables. Staged plist comment synced (`7e650a528c71`).
- **Verified** by `--dry-run` (syntax OK; correctly SKIP-active on Marie's live 184K/age-1m session; intra-day dedup hook ran report-mode = clean; no mutation, no send).
- **★ VERIFIED IN PRODUCTION (F26, real runtime, 6c.37 same-day).** Mid-session Marie hit a live compaction-timeout death-spiral (gateway err: context overflow 13:48 → repeated `compaction retry aggregate timeout (60000ms): proceeding with pre-compaction state` at 14:09/14:15/14:24/14:26 → `incomplete turn detected … surfacing error to user` = Peter's "⚠️ Agent couldn't generate a response"; the raw `Working… exec… tool: exec` leak). At **14:49** the scheduled reset **fired on its own at 179K** (age crossed 20m; the new 90K threshold + cooldown-clear), **archived** the 1.5MB stuck session to `agents/pa/sessions/archive/2026-07-16/933f91bc….jsonl` (recoverable), sent the **graceful heads-up** ("age=22m<=90m"), restarted the gateway → session absent = lean reload. Gateway healthy (pid 3909). So both the 90K threshold and the graceful notify are proven end-to-end in real runtime. **Gap it exposed → [P6-159]:** a *stuck* session reads `state=processing`, so the idle guard held it ~40m (96 timeouts logged) before it could fire — "stuck ≠ idle". Fixed in [P6-159].

### P6-156 — 6c.37: status-SLA + compaction-proof open-loops — DESIGNED (Peter-ratified) + BUILT inert; converts "never go silent on an active task" from failed prose ([P6-149]) into a host guarantee
**Type:** design-first (Peter-ratified) + reversible build (state file + host watcher + staged plist) · **6c.37** · £0 (dryrun-verified; no sends, no billed turns). openclaw.json untouched. The [P6-153] "★ status-SLA" now-win; the harm-reducer for the [P6-153] root #2 (engine keep-alive, Andreas).
- **State — `workspace-pa/memory/open-loops.json`** (`657c9cf769f5`/1158B): compaction-proof register (`id/what/who_waiting/opened_at/last_status_to_peter_at/next_action/status/sla_minutes`), seeded empty + self-documenting `_schema`. On disk ⇒ survives every compaction/reset (unlike working context).
- **Watcher — `scripts/open-loops-watch.sh`** (`84715da28689`/8116B, reply-watcher pattern): for any loop `active`/`waiting-external` whose silence exceeds its SLA it fires **once per SLA window** (re-arms only when `last_status_to_peter_at` advances or a full SLA re-elapses), **independent of the agent's context state**. Mode ladder: `dryrun` (default, £0) / `notify` (free) / `poke` (billed capped) / **`escalate`** (added 6c.37 = free heads-up to Peter + billed capped poke of Marie — Peter's ratified mode). **Dryrun tests PASS** (scratchpad fixture): SLA gating (active 45m fires; fresh/`waiting-external`-under-240m/`done` excluded), dedup (same status-ts suppressed), re-arm (advanced status-ts re-fires). Brief §62 wired (`AGENTS.md` `2721b4a909ff`): register a loop on pickup, advance the status-ts on every status, `done` on close — "the write is the acknowledgement".
- **Peter's 6c.37 decisions (AskUserQuestion):** mode = **escalate**; thresholds **active 45m / waiting-external 4h**. Staged plist (`286490b8ac14`/2903B) **pinned `dryrun`** for safe-bootstrap (reply-watcher precedent — escalate wakes Marie on **Opus**, billed, capped 4/day); recommended rollout = bootstrap dryrun → watch one real breach fire clean → flip `escalate`. **Peter bootstraps** (`launchctl` GUI/D20). poke primitive F26-proven ([P6-104], same `openclaw agent --deliver`) ⇒ no billed test required. `state/open-loops-watch.pa.*` will accrue on run.
- **Residual (honest):** enforcement depends on the loop being **registered** — tied to the `TASKS.md` reflex; reply-watcher + heartbeat still cover external-reply silence. Durable belt-and-braces (engine keep-alive) stays Andreas ([P6-153] root #2). Generalises to every agent unchanged.

### P6-159 — 6c.37: reset now also fires on a STUCK session (compaction-timeout spiral), not only an idle one — closes the "stuck ≠ idle" gap that [P6-155]'s production incident exposed
**Type:** reversible build (script edit) · **6c.37 (built at Peter's go, same session)** · £0 (replay + negative tests on real log data; no billed turns). openclaw.json untouched. Direct fix for the gap surfaced in [P6-155]'s F26 incident.
- **The gap.** The chat-bloat-reset guard required `idle≥20m`, treating `state=processing` as "live turn, don't interrupt". But a session stuck in the compaction-timeout spiral ([P6-129] 60s-timeout, no knob) keeps `updatedAt` fresh → it read as active every poll and thrashed ~40m (13:48→14:26, 96 timeouts) before it finally went idle and reset at 14:49. The reset couldn't rescue a *live-stuck* session, only an idle one.
- **The fix.** `scripts/chat-bloat-reset.sh` (`3a7bd2f71c15`→**`e4a6bd9a4b40`**/8806B): a **stuck-spiral detector** in the verdict logic tails the last ~400KB of `logs/gateway.err.log` and counts `compaction retry aggregate timeout` lines carrying THIS session's `sessionId=<sessionFile-basename>` within `CHAT_STUCK_WINDOW_MIN` (10m); if `≥ CHAT_STUCK_TIMEOUTS` (3) it declares the session **stuck** and **overrides ONLY the idle guard** — bloat (`tokens≥RESET_TOKENS`) and cooldown (`≥120m`, the restart-loop breaker) still hold. Live next 900s tick, **no restart**.
- **Verified on real log data (4 cases):** (1) **replay** — fixture "active" session (age 1m) + the real 933f91bc spiral, window 60 → `RESET STUCK-SPIRAL spiral=4>=3 … idle-guard overridden` (would have reset ~14:19 vs the actual 14:49 = ~30m saved); (2) **recovered state** — same fixture, default 10m window (spiral now >25m old) → `SKIP active stuck=0<3` (no false-fire); (3) **healthy active** — no timeouts → `SKIP active stuck=0<3` (never interrupts a genuine long turn); (4) **idle+bloated** — normal path unchanged → `RESET … stuck=0`. Conservative by construction: a real spiral is unambiguous, a healthy turn produces zero timeout markers.
- **Still a harm-reducer, not the root.** This recovers her faster; the durable cure (no bloat → no spiral) is the Andreas frozen-core brief-slice ([P6-153] root #1). Generalises: any agent whose session logs the same spiral would be caught (pa-scoped today by the script's KEY).
